 centre sarkaar ke 29 vibhaagon ne in 598 samasyaon kii pahchaan kii he, jinamein hawaonddon kii jeeyo-fensing, online toll collection, smart trephic management, sible hamale tathaa hawaikshetra ko surakshit banane ke liye smart drone bhi shaamil hai
 The digital programming competition, which runs continuously for 36 hours, will start from 26 am on Saturday at 26 different places in the country
 har jagah par hekathon kii jimmedaari ek kendriya vibhaag yaa mantralay kii hogi
 The top three teams will be awarded Rs 1 lakh, Rs 75,000 and Rs 50,000 and will use digital solutions to improve the ministry / department governance system
 puraskaar paane vaale sabhi vijetaon ko community of innovative minds main shaamil kiya jayega
 The Hackathon also aims to improve the awareness of patents in the country
 world intlexual property organijeshan (dablyooipo) ke mutabik, bharat main prati 10 lakh kii aabaadi main 40 patent hota he

 The world's largest hakathon, 'smart India Hackathon' will start from 26 places in the country from Saturday
 'smart india hekathon' ke bare main kaha ja rahaa he ki yah duniya kaa sabase bada hekathon he
 According to a release issued by the Ministry of Electronics and Information Technology, the aim of this hackathon is to promote innovation, in which about 10,000 students will be seen to solve 598 problems digitally
 centre sarkaar ke 29 vibhaagon ne in 598 samasyaon kii pahchaan kii he, jinamein hawaonddon kii jeeyo-fensing, online toll collection, smart trephic management, sible hamale tathaa hawaikshetra ko surakshit banane ke liye smart drone bhi shaamil hai
 The digital programming competition, which runs continuously for 36 hours, will start from 26 am on Saturday at 26 different places in the country
 har jagah par hekathon kii jimmedaari ek kendriya vibhaag yaa mantralay kii hogi
 The top three teams will be awarded Rs 1 lakh, Rs 75,000 and Rs 50,000 and will use digital solutions to improve the ministry / department governance system
 puraskaar paane vaale sabhi vijetaon ko community of innovative minds main shaamil kiya jayega
 The Hackathon also aims to improve the awareness of patents in the country

 ) lagaataar 36 ghante tak chalane vaali digital programing pratiyogita shanivaar ko subah aath baje se desh kii 26 vibhinn jagahon par shuru hogi

 sheersh teen tiimon ko ek lakh rupee, 75,000 rupee tathaa 50,000 rupee se puraskrit kiya jayega or digital solutions kaa istemaal mantralay / vibhaag shashan pranali kaa sudhaar karne ke liye karegaa
 All winners of the award will be included in the Community of Innovative Minds
 hekathon kaa uddeshy desh main patent ke bare main jaagrukta main sudhaar karnaa bhi he

 Air India Air Transport Services Limited (AIATSL) has held 64 security agents positions
 bataa den, chune gaye ummidavaargova airportke liye niyukt kiye jaaenge
 At the same time, the contract for this post will be three years
 eietisel vaikency ke liye walk-in-intervyuu main bhaag lene kii aakhri taarikh 29 or 30 sitambar 2018 he
 Know who can apply: For the post of Security Agents, the candidate has obtained a degree of graduation from a recognized institution / university with the ability to communicate with Hindi, English and local language from a recognized institution
 iske alaava, ummidavaar ke paas BCAS basic AVSEC (12 din kaa nayaa pattern) hona chahie
 Other information: Candidates who are AVSEC have maximum age of 31 years and without AVSEC, the age of those candidates should not be more than 28 years
 likhit pariksha orintervyuke aadhaar par chayan kiya jayega
 The selected candidates will be given Rs 18,360

 Interview time is from 9 am to 2 pm

 Interview time is from 7 am to 11 pm
 pienbi mahaghotaale kii paraten jaise-jaise khul rahi hai, isamen tamaam nai-nai jaankariyaan saamne aa rahi hai
 The Enforcement Directorate has registered a case against the bank and diamond businessman Nirav Modi and several of his associates in connection with the fraud of about Rs 11,000 crore in Punjab National Bank
 pravartan nideshaalay ke sutron ke anusaar neerav or unki sahyogi companiyon ko bank ne ansikyord lone die or bank adhikari unki sahyogi companiyon se bhi nirantar sampark main the
 What is Unsecured Loan: Unsecured loan is called when the bank gives loan without any security or collateral
 isamen lone karj lene vaale kii haisiyat, karj chukaane kii kshamta ke aadhaar par hi de diya jaataa he
 An ED source said, "the firm of Nirav Modi and his associate companies were given unsecured loans
 yahi nahin, bank adhikari nirantar neerav kii sahyogi companiyon ke saath sampark main the
 The bank gave loan without any security
 is jaalsaji kaa khulaasa tab jaakar hua jab neerav karj lautaane main vifal rahe
 How was it? An employee of a Mumbai branch of fraudulent NNB used to provide letter of undertaking (LOU) to diamond companies to secure securitized overseas loans from other banks
 rajeev kumaar ne bataaya, 'hira company yah aloyu kisi anya bhartiya bank kii videshi shakha ko detii thi
 The entire forgery is about Rs 11,400 crore
 ' pienbi se hasil is aloyu ke aadhaar par hi union bank of india, elahabaad bank, exis bank aadi nehira companiyonko karj diya
 But to avoid being caught, PNB employees did not enter the LOU in the bank's register
 sutron ke anusaar pienbi ke aloyu parunion bankne 2,300 karod rupee, elahabaad bank ne 2,000 karod rupee or esbiai ne 960 karod rupee kaa lone diya

 The Supreme Court refused to stay the order of the Andhra Pradesh High Court to repeal the decision to grant reservation to minorities on the basis of religion in central educational institutions
 supreme court ke is rukh ke baad bhartiya praudyogiki santhaan (iaiti) jaisi pratishthit kendriya shikshan sansthaaon main alpsankhyakon ke liye 4
 As many as 325 students who had expected admission under the 5 per cent reservation system, were left disappointed
 nyaayamurti kees radhakrishnan or nyaayamurti jees khehad kii avkaashkaleen peeth ne atirikt solicytor general gaurav banerjee kii daleelein sunne ke baad do took shabdon me kaha, ham hoicourt ke aadesh par roak nahin lagaayenge
 The judges questioned the government that out of the reservation of other backward classes, can such classification be done on the basis of religion? nyaayadhishon ne iske saath hi maanav sansaadhan vikaas mantralay kii yachika par aar krishnamaiya tathaa un duusare prativaadiyon ko notice jari kiye, jinaki yachika par anya pichde varg ke 27 fisadi cote main se alpsankhyakon ke liye 4
 The provision of 5 per cent reservation was repealed by the High Court
 is maamle kii sunwaayee shuru hote hi nyaayadhishon ne kaha ki centre sarkaar ne alpsankhyakon ke liye aarakshan ke paksh main unke samaksh badi sankhya main dastavej pesh kiye hai
 It would have been more logical to present these documents in the High Court
 atirikt solicytor general gaurav banerjee ne is par kaha ki ucch nyaayalay ko yah lag rahaa tha ki ye aarakshan shaayad sabhi alpsankhyakon ke liye he
 To this, the judges said, "this is the same feeling from the memorandum of office about reservation"
 banerjee ne kaha ki buddha or parsi samudaay jaise alpsankhyak 4
 5 percent is not included in the reservation list
 unhone kaha ki dharmik alpsankhyak samudaay anya pichde virgon ke liye nirdhaarit 27 fisadi aarakshan ke daayre main shaamil hai, jabaki 4
 Reservation of this part of 5 per cent includes the lowest strata or Muslim converting Christians of Muslim society
 nyaayadhishon kaa kahana tha ki 4
 The office memorandum issued on December 22, 2011 regarding 5 per cent reservation did not even receive any legislative support
 anya pichde virgon ke 27 fisadi aarakshan main se 4
 Questioning the calculation of 5 percent reservation, the judges wanted to know whether this reservation has the support of any constitutional or legislative body? The judges also wanted to know whether 4
 5 fisadi aarakshan sambandhi karyaalay gyaapan ko koi sanvidhanik yaa vidhaayi samarthan praapt he? Gaurav Banerjee could not give any satisfactory answer to these questions
 unhone nyaayadhishon se baar-baar yah anurodh kiya ki iaiti main pravesh ke liye ho rahi counselling ke maddenjar ucch nyaayalay ke aadesh par roak lagaai jaae, kyonki 4
 a list of 325 students of this class has been prepared under the 5% reservation quota
 lekin nyaayadhish unki in daleelon se prabhavit nahin hue or unhone kaha ki ve anya pichde virgon ke 27 fisadi aarakshan main se alpsankhyakon ko 4
 The decision to grant 5 per cent reservation will not be stayed by the decision
 tippaniyan On May 28, the High Court had declared the provision of reservation for minorities unconstitutional
 iske baad hi maanav sansaadhan vikaas mantralay ne ucchtam nyaayalay kaa darwaja khatkhataya tha
 4 from the Ministry of Human Resource Development on June 11 by the Supreme Court
 5 fisadi aarakshan se jude saare tathy or dastavej maange the
 The court had also made clear on that day that the government should not have taken up such a complex and sensitive issue in this way
 yahi nahin, sheersh adaalat ne is visham sthiti ke liye ucch nyaayalay par dosha madhne ke centre sarkaar ke ravaiye par naaraazgi bhi jaahir kii thi
